His work contributed significantly to the Christianization and cultural development of the region.

One of his major contributions was his advocacy for education. He founded schools and brought in scholars, fostering an environment where learning and intellectual inquiry were highly valued. This was a significant step in the development of the educational foundation of the region, which would have lasting impacts on its cultural and intellectual growth.

Vergilius also played a crucial role in missionary work, continuing the efforts to spread Christianity throughout the area, particularly among the pagan populations. His work in consolidating the church's presence and organizing its structure was vital for the stability and growth of the Christian community in the region.

Moreover, Vergilius was involved in a famous controversy related to his teachings, which some saw as heretical because he proposed the existence of antipodes – people living on the opposite side of the Earth. This view was controversial at the time because it challenged the existing theological understanding of the world. However, Vergilius defended his views, and eventually, Pope Zachary confirmed his orthodoxy, allowing him to continue his work without ecclesiastical censure.

His legacy is not just tied to his missionary and educational efforts but also to his forward-thinking views on science and the world, showcasing a blend of faith and reason that was ahead of his time. Vergilius of Salzburg is remembered as a key figure in the Christianization and cultural development of the region, and his contributions have had a lasting impact on the Church and education in what is now Austria.

Following a thorough examination, Pope Zachary validated Vergilius's orthodoxy, enabling him to persist with his work unimpeded. Vergilius's legacy extends beyond his educational and missionary achievements; he is also recognized for his prescient scientific viewpoints, encapsulating a unique fusion of faith and reason that preceded his era. Vergilius of Salzburg is revered as a critical figure in both the Christianization and cultural progression of the region, his contributions leaving an indelible mark on both the Church and education in present-day Austria.

In remembrance, Vergilius of Salzburg stands as a significant personality in the Christianization and cultural enhancement of the territory, his contributions indelibly shaping the Church and education within modern Austria.
